<a class="teaser__link" href="/en/2027/news-press-releases/278543.html" title="" target="_self">
<h2 class="teaser__title">Current Funding Recommendations</h2>
</a>
<p>At the 43rd jury session of the <i>Berlinale World Cinema Fund</i>, the jury made nine funding recommendations, allocating the current funding to projects from Bangladesh, Burkina Faso, Cambodia, Ecuador, Lebanon, Malaysia, Philippines, Senegal, and Turkey. Additionally, three German cinema releases have been supported.</p>
</div>

<a class="teaser__link" href="/en/2027/news-press-releases/278538.html" title="" target="_self">
<h2 class="teaser__title">In Memory of Moritz de Hadeln</h2>
</a>
<p>With the passing of Moritz de Hadeln, the international film community has lost one of its most influential and respected figures. As a festival director, filmmaker, and passionate advocate for cinema, he played a pivotal role in shaping European and international film culture over several decades.</p>
</div>
</div>

<p class="teaser__category">News | European Film Market</p>
<a class="teaser__link" href="/en/2027/news-press-releases/278472.html" title="Berlinale News" target="_self">
<h2 class="teaser__title">South Africa to be Celebrated as <i>EFM</i>&rsquo;s &ldquo;Country in Focus&rdquo; at the Berlinale 2027</h2>
</a>
<p>As one of Africa&rsquo;s most globally integrated and diversified economies, South Africa is home to a dynamic and internationally connected film industry that combines creative excellence, strong production capabilities and growing global market relevance.</p>
</div>
